## Instruction

Please read the content from [https://www.when2meet.com/?22412161-cUzZy](https://www.when2meet.com/?22412161-cUzZy) and summarize the information, providing each person's available time slots. Analyze team members' calendar availability and automatically recommend one 2-hour weekly meeting slot. Send the schedule arrangement to meeting administrator [jjones@mcp.com](mailto:jjones@mcp.com). The email content should include the meeting time (in a format like "Monday 9:00 AM to 11:00 AM every week") and the names of all participants. You need to follow the content format in `format.md`.

}

def analyze_availability():
    # Calculate availability for each time slot
    slot_availability = defaultdict(list)
    
    for person_id, available_slots in availability.items():
        for slot_idx in available_slots:
            slot_availability[slot_idx].append(person_id)
    
    # Find best 2-hour consecutive slots (8 slots = 2 hours, as each slot is 15 minutes)
    best_slots = []
    max_people = 0
    
    for start_slot in range(len(time_slots) - 7):  # Need 8 consecutive slots for 2 hours
        consecutive_slots = range(start_slot, start_slot + 8)
        
        # Find people available for ALL 8 consecutive slots
        available_people = set(slot_availability[consecutive_slots[0]])
        for slot_idx in consecutive_slots[1:]:
            available_people = available_people.intersection(set(slot_availability[slot_idx]))
        
        if len(available_people) > max_people:
            max_people = len(available_people)
            best_slots = [(start_slot, available_people)]
        elif len(available_people) == max_people and len(available_people) > 0:
            best_slots.append((start_slot, available_people))
    
    return best_slots, max_people

def format_time_slot(timestamp):
    dt = datetime.datetime.fromtimestamp(timestamp, tz=datetime.timezone.utc)
    return dt.strftime("%A %I:%M %p")

def get_day_from_timestamp(timestamp):
    dt = datetime.datetime.fromtimestamp(timestamp, tz=datetime.timezone.utc)
    return dt.strftime("%A")

# Analyze and find best meeting times
best_slots, max_people = analyze_availability()

print("HKUST NLP Group Meeting Availability Analysis")
print("=" * 50)
print(f"Total participants: {len(people_names)}")
print(f"Maximum people available for 2-hour slots: {max_people}")
print()

print("RECOMMENDED 2-HOUR MEETING SLOTS:")
print("-" * 40)

for i, (start_slot, available_people) in enumerate(best_slots[:5]):  # Show top 5 options
    start_time = time_slots[start_slot]
    end_time = time_slots[start_slot + 7]  # 8 slots = 2 hours
    
    start_formatted = format_time_slot(start_time)
    end_formatted = format_time_slot(end_time)
    day = get_day_from_timestamp(start_time)
    
    print(f"{i+1}. {day} {datetime.datetime.fromtimestamp(start_time, tz=datetime.timezone.utc).strftime('%I:%M %p')} to {datetime.datetime.fromtimestamp(end_time, tz=datetime.timezone.utc).strftime('%I:%M %p')} ({max_people}/{len(people_names)} people available)")
    
    available_names = [people_names[pid] for pid in available_people]
    print(f"   Available: {', '.join(sorted(available_names))}")
    print()

# Show individual availability summary
print("\nINDIVIDUAL AVAILABILITY SUMMARY:")
print("-" * 40)
for person_id, name in people_names.items():
    available_count = len(availability.get(person_id, []))
    total_slots = len(time_slots)
    percentage = (available_count / total_slots) * 100
    print(f"{name}: {available_count}/{total_slots} slots ({percentage:.1f}%)")

i < timeSlots.length; i++) {\n            slotAvailability[i] = availableAtSlot[i] || [];\n        }\n        \n        // Find best 2-hour consecutive slots (8 slots = 2 hours, as each slot is 15 minutes)\n        let bestSlots = [];\n        let maxPeople = 0;\n        \n        for (let startSlot = 0; startSlot < timeSlots.length - 7; startSlot++) {\n            // Find people available for ALL 8 consecutive slots\n            let availablePeople = new Set(slotAvailability[startSlot]);\n            \n            for (let i = 1; i < 8; i++) {\n                const slotPeople = new Set(slotAvailability[startSlot + i]);\n                availablePeople = new Set([...availablePeople].filter(x => slotPeople.has(x)));\n            }\n            \n            if (availablePeople.size > maxPeople) {\n                maxPeople = availablePeople.size;\n                bestSlots = [{startSlot, availablePeople: [...availablePeople]}];\n            } else if (availablePeople.size === maxPeople && availablePeople.size > 0) {\n                bestSlots.push({startSlot, availablePeople: [...availablePeople]});\n            }\n        }\n        \n        // Format results\n        function formatTimeSlot(timestamp) {\n            const dt = new Date(timestamp * 1000);\n            return dt.toLocaleString(\'en-US\', {\n                weekday: \'long\',\n                hour: \'numeric\',\n                minute: \'2-digit\',\n                hour12: true,\n                timeZone: \'UTC\'\n            });\n        }\n        \n        console.log("HKUST NLP Group Meeting Availability Analysis");\n        console.log("=" + "=".repeat(50));\n        console.log("Total participants:", peopleNames.length);\n        console.log("Maximum people available for 2-hour slots:", maxPeople);\n        console.log("");\n        \n        console.log("RECOMMENDED 2-HOUR MEETING SLOTS:");\n        console.log("-".repeat(40));\n        \n        window.meetingAnalysis = {\n            maxPeople,\n            bestSlots: bestSlots.slice(0, 5),\n            timeSlots,\n            peopleNames,\n            peopleIDs\n        };\n        \n        for (let i = 0;
